    SELECT TOP(1) [a].[Id], [a].[Email], [a].[Phone], [a].[RoleId], [a].[UserPhotoId], [a].[Username], [a].[Verify], [p].[Id] AS [Id0], [p].[Account_Id], [p].[PasswordValue], [r].[Id] AS [Id1], [r].[Name]
    FROM [Accounts] AS [a]
    LEFT JOIN [Passwords] AS [p] ON [a].[Id] = [p].[Account_Id]
    INNER JOIN [Roles] AS [r] ON [a].[RoleId] = [r].[Id]
    WHERE [a].[Email] = @__email_0
) AS [t]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [r0].[RoleId], [r0].[PermissionId], [r0].[Id], [p0].[Id] AS [Id0], [p0].[Action]
    FROM [RolesPermissions] AS [r0]
    INNER JOIN [Permissions] AS [p0] ON [r0].[PermissionId] = [p0].[Id]
) AS [t0] ON [t].[Id1] = [t0].[RoleId]
ORDER BY [t].[Id], [t].[Id0], [t].[Id1], [t0].[RoleId], [t0].[PermissionId]
